				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					The Planets, Op.32 (Holst, Gustav)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th>Incipit
</th>
<td>7 movements <div class="expandline" style="background-color:#E8E8E8;margin-left:0;margin-top:0;padding:0">
<ol><li> Mars: <img src="/images/lilypond/e446dbcb2c887f54a04256f463b807d4.png" alt="\relative c { \clef bass \time 5/4 \key c \major \tempo &quot;Allegro&quot; \tuplet 3/2 { g8_\markup { \dynamic p \italic &quot;col ligno&quot; } g g } g4 g g8 g g4 \bar &quot;:|]&quot; }" />
</li><li> Venus: <img src="/images/lilypond/5767aacddef0527b6884d5a8fe23e9b5.png" alt="\new StaffGroup { &lt;&lt; \new Staff \with { instrumentName = &quot;Flute I/II&quot; } \relative c''' { \time 4/4 \tempo &quot;Adagio&quot; \clef treble \key ees \major R1*2 | r4 &lt;ees g>\p\>( &lt;d f> &lt;bes d> | &lt;aes c>2 &lt;g bes>\! | aes8 ) r r4 r2 } \new Staff \with { instrumentName = &quot;Horn I&quot; } \relative c'' { \time 4/4 \tempo &quot;Adagio&quot; \clef treble \transposition f \key c \major c2\p\>( d4 ees | f1 ) | c2\p\>( d4 ees | f4. ) r8\! r2 | R1 } >> }" />
</li><li> Mercury: <img src="/images/lilypond/6cdd375fcb2aa7553c18d234cdde0dcf.png" alt="\relative c' { \key c \major \time 6/8 \tempo &quot;Vivace&quot; \clef treble f8( bes d e b gis ) | a'( e cis ) e( b gis ) }" />

</td></tr>

</td></tr>

</li><li> Venus, the Bringer of Peace. Adagio 
</li><li> Mercury, the Winged Messenger. Vivace
</li><li> Jupiter, the Bringer of Jollity. Allegro giocoso
</li><li> Saturn, the Bringer of Old Age. Adagio
</li><li> Uranus, the Magician. Allegro
</li><li> Neptune, the Mystic. Andante

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Extra Information
</th>
<td>Conceived as a work for piano duet or organ, but premiered as a work for large orchestra.
</td></tr></table>
